5. Reprofile and next primitive: close or record rejection, sync/push, then name the next deeper alien primitive and target ratio.
6. Eigensolver scalar norm probe: test the QL hot-loop `eigh_pythag` direct-square lever and reject it unless same-worker full/vector residual wins clear noise and no values-only regression appears.
7. Full-eigh structural lever: attack residual memory movement around full-vector tridiagonal solve/sort/copy without changing QL rotation order, eigenvalue ordering, or eigenvector orientation.
8. Reprofile deeper primitive: update the no-gaps blocked tridiagonalization / tridiagonal D&C plan with the next measured target ratio after the pass-7 keep/reject gate.
9. Back-transform row-parallel probe: test the independent row-update fan-out and reject unless same-worker full-eigh improves without values-only pollution.

11. BLAS-3 trailing update gate: benchmark a lower-triangle rank-2k update helper against the scalar trailing update on the measured 256x256 residual.
12. Strict-mode fallback ledger: route blocked dsytrd only under an explicit mode/size gate until ordering, sign, and FP reassociation ledgers pass.
13. Tridiagonal solver reprofile: re-measure after blocked-reduction work and choose between secular D&C and QL vector-rotation replacement.
14. ft-serialize native decode reprofile: baseline the many-small f64 native state-dict decode hotspot and select one profile-backed decode primitive.
15. Decode isomorphism proof: preserve BTreeMap ordering, duplicate-key, truncation, UTF-8 error, dtype, shape, and f64 raw-bit semantics with golden SHA-256 evidence.
16. Same-worker rebench gate: keep only a same-worker Criterion win with Score >= 2.0 and record rejection otherwise.
17. Reprofile after ft-serialize closeout: check the next ready perf bead or file a disjoint profile-backed fallback target.
18. Deeper primitive routing: if micro-levers fail, harvest the next zero-copy/blocked/SIMD primitive from alien-graveyard and alien-artifact proof workflow.
19. Pinv QR full-rank fast path: replace the measured no-grad SVD rectangular pseudo-inverse hotspot with a conservative Q-free Householder QR primitive.
20. Reprofile after pinv closeout: pick the next ready `[perf]` bead or file a profile-backed independent target.
21. Optimizer arena/SoA primitive: if optimizer remains hot, attack region/slab workspace or batched vectorized state layout with allocation counters.
22. Recurrent raw-kernel primitive: if sequence kernels surface, target no-grad packed gate/state kernels with exact ordering and gradient isolation.
